Source Code

This source code is very close to the Apollo Guidance Computer software for the Apollo 13 Lunar module. This revision of the Luminary 131 program is from December of 1969, whereas there was a later revision in January of 1970, and still another revision in February, which is the code that flew on the mission. As far as this transcription is concerned, it was originally from a copy made in 1991 of a printout from the collection of AGC developer Don Eyles for collector David Craig. It was subsequently scanned by Gary Neff, reprocessed for online presentation at the now-discontinued History of Recent Science and Technology (HRST) website of MIT's Dibner Institute (the full-quality scans being discarded in the process), and finally transcribed by Ron Burkey for the Virtual AGC Project. Although a high-quality replacement scan for a completely illegible page was later provided by Gary Neff, the reduced legibility of the reprocessed HRST posting nevertheless caused many errors to be introduced into the transcription. Accordingly, a second scan of the same physical printout was made in 2017 for the Virtual AGC Project's collection at the Internet Archive, and used to correct the transcription errors. All of the scanned materials mentioned, as well as other Luminary 131 related material, are available online. Don Eyles apprently made additional hand-written notes in printout between 1991 and 2017, so the two scans are not identical in that respect. The page-headings in the printout read, in part:
	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 131 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-091
	17:53 DEC. 19, 1969
Note that the date is the date the printout was made, not the date on which the program revision was released, although these happen to be very close together. 

020986,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
020987,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
020988,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary 1C, revision 131.
020989,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the Lunar Module's (LM)
020990,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 13.
020991,000007:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except
020992,000008:                                                                                                  ##              that the code format has been changed to conform to the
020993,000009:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the 
020994,000010:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.
020995,000011:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 496-618
020996,000012:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
020997,000013:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
020998,000014:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 05/15/03 RSB.   Began transcribing.

021000,000016:                                                                                                  ##                              the bottom of p. 595 using a replacement scan
021001,000017:                                                                                                  ##                              provided by Gary Neff.
021002,000018:                                                                                                  ##              05/14/05 RSB    Corrected website reference above.

021013,000029:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
021014,000030: 
021015,000031:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021016,000032: 
021017,000033:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021018,000034:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021019,000035: 
021020,000036:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021021,000037: 
021022,000038:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
021023,000039:                                                                                                  #        STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
021024,000040:                                                                                                  #        THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
021025,000041:                                                                                                  #        ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
021026,000042: 
021027,000043:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021028,000044: 
021029,000045:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
021030,000046: 
021031,000047:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021032,000048: 
021033,000049:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      FLAGUP
021034,000050:                                                                                                  #        GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                       FLAGDOWN
021035,000051:                                                                                                  #        R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)                    BANKCALL
021036,000052:                                                                                                  #        LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)                     TASKOVER
021037,000053:                                                                                                  #        LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
021038,000054:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
021039,000055:                                                                                                  #        R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                          ENDOFJOB
021040,000056:                                                                                                  #        R22LEM  (DATA READ)                             GOPERF1
021041,000057:                                                                                                  #        R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)  
021042,000058:                                                                                                  #        PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
021043,000059: 
021044,000060:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021045,000061: 
021046,000062:                                                                                                  #        P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS - ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021047,000063:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
021048,000064: 
021049,000065:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021050,000066: 
021051,000067:                                                                                                  #        RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
021052,000068: 
021053,000069:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021054,000070: 
021055,000071:                                                                                                  #        TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
021056,000072: 
021057,000073:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021058,000074: 
021059,000075:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021060,000076: 
021061,000077:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, RNDVZFLG, ACMODFLG, VEHUPFLG, UPDATFLG, TRACKFLG,
021062,000078: 
021063,000079:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021064,000080: 
021065,000081:                                                                                                  #        CENTRALS - A,Q,L
021066,000082: 
021067,000083: 25,2073  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
021068,000084: 
021069,000085: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
021070,000086: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
021071,000087: 24,2000                                           BANK

021481,000497:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021482,000498: 
021483,000499:                                                                                                  #        PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
021484,000500:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 3
021485,000501:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021486,000502: 
021487,000503:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021488,000504: 
021489,000505:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
021490,000506:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
021491,000507:                                                                                                  #        CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
021492,000508:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
021493,000509: 
021494,000510:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021495,000511: 
021496,000512:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
021497,000513: 
021498,000514:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021499,000515: 
021500,000516:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL                                        FLAGUP
021501,000517:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      ENDOFJOB
021502,000518:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)                     WAITLIST
021503,000519:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER                                        FINDVAC
021504,000520: 
021505,000521:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021506,000522: 
021507,000523:                                                                                                  #        P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS - ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021508,000524:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E

021570,000586:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
021571,000587:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021572,000588: 
021573,000589:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021574,000590:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
021575,000591: 
021576,000592:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021577,000593: 
021578,000594:                                                                                                  #        TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
021579,000595:                                                                                                  #        LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
021580,000596: 
021581,000597:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021582,000598: 
021583,000599:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021584,000600:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R22LEM
021585,000601: 
021586,000602:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021587,000603: 
021588,000604:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.1         GOFLASH         WAITLIST
021589,000605:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.2         PRIOLARM        BANKCALL
021590,000606:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.3         R61LEM
021591,000607: 
021592,000608:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021593,000609: 
021594,000610:                                                                                                  #        R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE, UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA
021595,000611:                                                                                                  #        UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME

021790,000806:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
021791,000807:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021792,000808: 
021793,000809:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021794,000810:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
021795,000811: 
021796,000812:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021797,000813: 
021798,000814:                                                                                                  #        TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
021799,000815:                                                                                                  #        OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR.  ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
021800,000816: 
021801,000817:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021802,000818: 
021803,000819:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021804,000820:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R21LEM
021805,000821: 
021806,000822:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021807,000823: 
021808,000824:                                                                                                  #        FINDVAC         FLAGUP          ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
021809,000825:                                                                                                  #        NOVAC           INTPRET         LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
021810,000826:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        JOBSLEEP        JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
021811,000827:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER        BANKCALL        RADSTALL        RRDESSM
021812,000828: 
021813,000829:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
021814,000830:                                                                                                  #        
021815,000831:                                                                                                  #        WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED, BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
021816,000832:                                                                                                  #        WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER (BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
021817,000833: 
021818,000834:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021819,000835: 
021820,000836:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
021821,000837:                                                                                                  #        THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
021822,000838:                                                                                                  #        ACQUISITION
021823,000839: 
021824,000840:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021825,000841: 
021826,000842:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM
021827,000843: 
021828,000844:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021829,000845: 
021830,000846:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
021831,000847: 
021832,000848:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021833,000849: 
021834,000850:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        LOKONSW
021835,000851: 
021836,000852:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021837,000853: 
021838,000854:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRSESSM
021839,000855: 
021840,000856: 24,2675  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021841,000857: 24,2675                                           COUNT*   $$/R21

021843,000859: 24,2676           00006                           EXTEND

022016,001032:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM
022017,001033:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022018,001034: 
022019,001035:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022020,001036:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
022021,001037: 
022022,001038:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022023,001039: 
022024,001040:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022025,001041: 
022026,001042:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022027,001043: 
022028,001044:                                                                                                  #        TC      R23LEM
022029,001045: 
022030,001046:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022031,001047: 
022032,001048:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL        R61LEM
022033,001049:                                                                                                  #        SETMINDB        GOPERF1
022034,001050: 
022035,001051:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022036,001052: 
022037,001053:                                                                                                  #        IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1      ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
022038,001054:                                                                                                  #                                        ,SELECTION OF PROC WILL CONTINUE R23
022039,001055:                                                                                                  #                                        ,SELECTION OF TERM WILL TERMINATE R23 + P20
022040,001056: 
022041,001057:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022042,001058: 
022043,001059:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022044,001060: 
022045,001061:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022046,001062: 
022047,001063:                                                                                                  #        N.A.
022048,001064: 
022049,001065:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED -
022050,001066: 
022051,001067:                                                                                                  #        ACMODFLG MUST BE SET TO 1 (MANUAL MODE)

022100,001116:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
022101,001117:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022102,001118: 
022103,001119:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022104,001120:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
022105,001121: 
022106,001122:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022107,001123: 
022108,001124:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
022109,001125:                                                                                                  #        FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
022110,001126:                                                                                                  #        THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
022111,001127: 
022112,001128:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
022113,001129: 
022114,001130:                                                                                                  #        CAF     PRIONN
022115,001131:                                                                                                  #        TC      FINDVAC
022116,001132:                                                                                                  #        EBANK=  DATAGOOD
022117,001133:                                                                                                  #        2CADR   R24LEM
022118,001134: 
022119,001135:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022120,001136: 
022121,001137:                                                                                                  #        FLAGUP          FLAGDOWN        BANKCALL
022122,001138:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM          GOFLASHR        FINDVAC
022123,001139:                                                                                                  #        ENDOFJOB        NOVAC           LSR24.1
022124,001140: 
022125,001141:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022126,001142: 
022127,001143:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.  HE CAN EITHER
022128,001144:                                                                                                  #        REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
022129,001145:                                                                                                  #        PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
022130,001146: 
022131,001147:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022132,001148: 
022133,001149:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022134,001150: 
022135,001151:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
022136,001152: 
022137,001153:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
022138,001154: 
022139,001155:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022140,001156: 
022141,001157:                                                                                                  #        SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
022142,001158: 
022143,001159:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022144,001160: 
022145,001161:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, ACMODFLG
022146,001162: 
022147,001163: 24,3210  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
022148,001164: 24,3210                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
022149,001165: 24,3210           05504        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
022150,001166: 24,3211           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
022151,001167: 24,3212           05516                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
022152,001168: 24,3213           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
022153,001169: 24,3214           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO                                  
022154,001170: 24,3215           55733                           TS       DATAGOOD                              #  ZERO OUT DATA INDICATOR
022155,001171: 24,3216           55734                           TS       OMEGAD                                #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022156,001172: 24,3217           55735                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022157,001173: 24,3220           05353        R24LEM2            TC       PHASCHNG                              
022158,001174: 24,3221           04022                           OCT      04022                                 
022159,001175: 24,3222           33255                           CAF      V16N80                                
022160,001176: 24,3223           04616                           TC       BANKCALL

022210,001226:                                                                                                  #  RRDESSM WILL RETURN TO CALLER

022216,001232:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM

022445,001461:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ RRLIMCHK                        ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
022446,001462: 
022447,001463:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022448,001464: 
022449,001465:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
022450,001466:                                                                                                  #        THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.  INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
022451,001467:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2.  THE CURRENT RR
022452,001468:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
022453,001469:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
022454,001470: 
022455,001471:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022456,001472:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN LIMITS,
022457,001473:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
022458,001474:                                                                                                  #        IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
022459,001475: 
022460,001476:                                                                                                  #        MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022461,001477:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN
022462,001478:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
022463,001479:                                                                                                  #        AND -125 (+235) DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
022464,001480:                                                                                                  #        TO L +3.
022465,001481: 
022466,001482:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022467,001483: 
022468,001484:                                                                                                  #        L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
022469,001485:                                                                                                  #        L  +1  ADRES  T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
022470,001486: 
022471,001487:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022472,001488: 
022473,001489:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
022474,001490:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
022475,001491:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT EBANK).
022476,001492: 
022477,001493:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_   MAGSUB
022478,001494: 
022479,001495:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022480,001496: 
022481,001497:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022482,001498: 
022483,001499:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         L + 2   (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022484,001500:                                                                                                  #                L + 3   (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)

022529,001545:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ SETTRKF                                                 . IF EITHER:
022530,001546: 
022531,001547:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022532,001548:                                                                                                  #        SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.              HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
022533,001549:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
022534,001550:                                                                                                  #        IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
022535,001551:                                                                                                  #        IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
022536,001552:                                                                                                  #                1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
022537,001553:                                                                                                  #                   AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
022538,001554:                                                                                                  #                2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
022539,001555:                                                                                                  #                   8,5)
022540,001556:                                                                                                  #                3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
022541,001557:                                                                                                  #        THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
022542,001558:                                                                                                  #        IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
022543,001559:                                                                                                  #        LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
022544,001560:                                                                                                  #        THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
022545,001561:                                                                                                  #        TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
022546,001562:                                                                                                  #                A) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU'S NOT BEING ZEROED.
022547,001563:                                                                                                  #                B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
022548,001564:                                                                                                  #                   EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
022549,001565:                                                                                                  #                C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
022550,001566:                                                                                                  #                   WITH EITHER THE AL
022551,001567:

022601,001617:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
022602,001618: 
022603,001619:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022604,001620: 
022605,001621:                                                                                                  #        RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
022606,001622:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
022607,001623:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
022608,001624:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE.  UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
022609,001625:                                                                                                  #        WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
022610,001626:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
022611,001627:                                                                                                  #        INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE
022612,001628:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7).  IF
022613,001629:                                                                                                  #        SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
022614,001630:                                                                                                  #        FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
022615,001631:                                                                                                  #        RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM.  IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
022616,001632:                                                                                                  #        TC TASKOVER.
022617,001633: 
022618,001634:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
022619,001635:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
022620,001636:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
022621,001637: 
022622,001638:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022623,001639: 
022624,001640:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, STATE
022625,001641: 
022626,001642:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
022627,001643: 
022628,001644:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022629,001645:                                                                                                  #        
022630,001646:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022631,001647: 
022632,001648:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
022633,001649: 
022634,001650:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
022635,001651: 
022636,001652: 24,3256                                           BANK     24                                    
022637,001653: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
022638,001654: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
022639,001655: 
022640,001656: 25,2073  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022641,001657: 25,2073                                           COUNT*   $$/RSUB

022650,001666:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
022651,001667: 
022652,001668:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022653,001669: 
022654,001670:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
022655,001671:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
022656,001672:                                                                                                  #        LAMP IF REQUIRED.  INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
022657,001673:                                                                                                  #        BIT 1) IS SET.  FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
022658,001674:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
022659,001675:                                                                                                  #        WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
022660,001676:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU'S
022661,001677:                                                                                                  #        TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES.  THE
022662,001678:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED.  THE
022663,001679:                                                                                                  #        CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
022664,001680:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES.  IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
022665,001681:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
022666,001682:                                                                                                  #        IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
022667,001683:                                                                                                  #        INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1.  SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
022668,001684:                                                                                                  #        SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
022669,001685: 
022670,001686:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  L  TC  RRZEROSB  (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
022671,001687: 
022672,001688:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022673,001689: 
022674,001690:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
022675,001691: 
022676,001692:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
022677,001693: 
022678,001694:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022679,001695: 
022680,001696:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022681,001697: 
022682,001698:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
022683,001699: 
022684,001700:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
022685,001701: 
022686,001702: 25,2102           00006        RRZEROSB           EXTEND

022689,001705: 25,2105           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.
022690,001706: 25,2106           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                #  TURN ON ZERO RR CDU
022691,001707: 25,2107           05221                           TC       FIXDELAY

022727,001743:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
022728,001744: 
022729,001745:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022730,001746: 
022731,001747:                                                                                                  #        DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022732,001748:                                                                                                  #        TO A SAFE POSITION.  INIITALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
022733,001749:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
022734,001750:                                                                                                  #        AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
022735,001751:                                                                                                  #        DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS.  THE RR
022736,001752:                                                                                                  #        TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
022737,001753:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING.  IN EITHER
022738,001754:                                                                                                  #        CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
022739,001755:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12).  RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
022740,001756:                                                                                                  #        TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
022741,001757:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
022742,001758:                                                                                                  #        MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED.  RRSONLY IS THEN
022743,001759:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
022744,001760:                                                                                                  #        -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
022745,001761:                                                                                                  #        REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
022746,001762:                                                                                                  #        FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
022747,001763:                                                                                                  #        REPOSRPT.  HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
022748,001764:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
022749,001765:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10).  IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES.  IF NOT PRESENT
022750,001766:                                                                                                  #        INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
022751,001767:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
022752,001768:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER.
022753,001769: 
022754,001770:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022755,001771: 
022756,001772:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
022757,001773:                                                                                                  #        NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
022758,001774: 
022759,001775:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022760,001776: 
022761,001777:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022762,001778: 
022763,001779:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022764,001780: 
022765,001781:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
022766,001782: 
022767,001783:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022768,001784: 
022769,001785:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022770,001786: 
022771,001787:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022772,001788: 
022773,001789:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES
022774,001790: 
022775,001791: 25,2140           02167        DORREPOS           TC       SETRRECR                              #  SET UP RR CDU ERROR COUNTERS.
022776,001792: 
022777,001793:                                                                                                  #  ALARM 501 DELETED IN DANCE 279 PER PCR 97.

022820,001836:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                 IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
022821,001837: 
022822,001838:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                               S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
022823,001839:                                                                                                  #        REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE.  IT DRIVES THE
022824,001840:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
022825,001841:                                                                                                  #        180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
022826,001842:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
022827,001843:                                                                                                  #        TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
022828,001844:                                                                                                  #        INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL.  ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
022829,001845:                                                                                                  #        AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS).  INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022830,001846:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED.  CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
022831,001847:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
022832,001848:                                                                                                  #        OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
022833,001849:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022834,001850:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN.  CONTROL IS AGAIN
022835,001851:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
022836,001852:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
022837,001853:                                                                                                  #        -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1.  RMODINV
022838,001854:                                                                                                  #        IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
022839,001855:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE.  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
022840,001856:                                                                                                  #        IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE.  THE PROGRAM
022841,001857:                                                                                                  #        THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
022842,001858: 
022843,001859:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022844,001860: 
022845,001861:                                                                                                  #        FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
022846,001862:                                                                                                  #        THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
022847,001863:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
022848,001864:                                                                                                  #        OTHER MODE.
022849,001865: 
022850,001866:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022851,001867: 
022852,001868:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022853,001869: 
022854,001870:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022855,001871: 
022856,001872:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)
022857,001873: 
022858,001874:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022859,001875: 
022860,001876:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022861,001877: 
022862,001878:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022863,001879: 
022864,001880:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  STDESIG
022865,001881: 
022866,001882: 25,2202           34740        REMODE             CAF      ANTENBIT                              #  DRIVE TRUNNION TO 0 (180)
022867,001883: 25,2203           70110                           MASK     RADMODES                              #  (ERROR COUNTER ALREADY ENABLED)

022916,001932:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_        RRTONLY, RRSONLY
022917,001933: 
022918,001934:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022919,001935: 
022920,001936:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
022921,001937:                                                                                                  #        RRMANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION.  IT DRIVES TO
022922,001938:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
022923,001939:                                                                                                  #        FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED.  IF BOTH EXIST,
022924,001940:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS).  THIS INDICATES
022925,001941:                                                                                                  #        THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
022926,001942:                                                                                                  #        WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
022927,001943:                                                                                                  #        REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11).  IF NONE
022928,001944:                                                                                                  #        OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
022929,001945:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  IF YES,
022930,001946:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS
022931,001947:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
022932,001948:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE SET = 0.  FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
022933,001949:                                                                                                  #        REPEATED.
022934,001950: 
022935,001951:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:     L-1     CAF     *ANGLE*         (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
022936,001952:                                                                                                  #                        L       TC      RRTONLY         (TRUNNION ONLY)
022937,001953:                                                                                                  #                        RRSONLY                         (SHAFT ONLY)
022938,001954:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
022939,001955:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
022940,001956: 
022941,001957:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022942,001958: 
022943,001959:                                                                                                  #        C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
022944,001960: 
022945,001961:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022946,001962: 
022947,001963:                                                                                                  #        FIXDELAY, REPOSRPT, MAGSUB, RROUT
022948,001964:

022950,001966: 
022951,001967:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022952,001968:

022954,001970: 
022955,001971:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_ REPOSRPT (REMODE AND REPOSITION FLAGS PRESENT - RADMODES
022956,001972:                                                                                                  #        BITS 14, 11)
022957,001973:                                                                                                  #        L+1 (ANGLE WITHIN ONE DEGREE OR RR OUT OF AUTO MODE)

023008,002024:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                          RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
023009,002025: 
023010,002026:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023011,002027: 
023012,002028:                                                                                                  #        RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
023013,002029:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTER SCALING.  RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
023014,002030:                                                                                                  #        GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
023015,002031:                                                                                                  #        TO THE DESIRED VALUES.  INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
023016,002032:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
023017,002033:                                                                                                  #        384 PULSES.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
023018,002034:                                                                                                  #        LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES.  THE DIFFERENCE IS
023019,002035:                                                                                                  #        THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
023020,002036:                                                                                                  #        THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
023021,002037:                                                                                                  #        THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
023022,002038:                                                                                                  #        PASS).  FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
023023,002039:                                                                                                  #        OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
023024,002040:                                                                                                  #        ARE SET.  THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023025,002041: 
023026,002042:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023027,002043:                                                                                                  #        
023028,002044:                                                                                                  #        L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
023029,002045:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES
023030,002046: 
023031,002047:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023032,002048: 
023033,002049:                                                                                                  #        TANG, TANG +1 (DESIRED COMMANDS), LASTYCMD, LASTXCMD
023034,002050:                                                                                                  #        (1ST PASS = 0), RR ERROR COUNTER ENAGLE SET (CHAN 12 BIT 2).
023035,002051:

023118,002134:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
023119,002135: 
023120,002136:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
023121,002137: 
023122,002138:                                                                                                  #        THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
023123,002139:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
023124,002140:                                                                                                  #        (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
023125,002141:                                                                                                  #        ORIENTATION.  INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
023126,002142:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
023127,002143:                                                                                                  #        MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
023128,002144:                                                                                                  #        RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
023129,002145:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
023130,002146:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
023131,002147:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS.  IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
023132,002148:                                                                                                  #        LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
023133,002149:                                                                                                  #        REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
023134,002150:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED.  FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
023135,002151:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
023136,002152:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
023137,002153:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS.  IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
023138,002154:                                                                                                  #        THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
023139,002155:                                                                                                  #        INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
023140,002156:                                                                                                  #        EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
023141,002157:                                                                                                  #        OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
023142,002158:                                                                                                  #        BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
023143,002159:                                                                                                  #        TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
023144,002160: 
023145,002161:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023146,002162: 
023147,002163:                                                                                                  #        L       STCALL  RRTARGET        (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
023148,002164:                                                                                                  #        L+1     RRDESSM
023149,002165:                                                                                                  #        L+2     BASIC                   (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023150,002166:                                                                                                  #        L+3     BASIC                   (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023151,002167: 
023152,002168:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023153,002169: 
023154,002170:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES
023155,002171: 
023156,002172:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023157,002173: 
023158,002174:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
023159,002175:                                                                                                  #        PART OF), RMODINV
023160,002176: 
023161,002177:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023162,002178: 
023163,002179:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023164,002180: 
023165,002181:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023166,002182: 
023167,002183:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
023168,002184:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE-RETURNS
023169,002185:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                 CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.
023170,002186: 
023171,002187: 25,2404           43020        RRDESSM            STQ      CLEAR                                 
023172,002188: 25,2405           01112                                    DESRET

023176,002192: 25,2410           47541                                    CDUTRIG
